  Colorado, Monday, June 18, 2018, @ 9:45 p.m. (MDT)—An witness who describes
  himself as an experienced pilot and aircraft mechanic, reports having witnessed
  a peculiar white light,
          <span class="SpellE">

          </span>
          by dark storm
  clouds.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>

  witness to wobble slightly, and after approximately 2-3 minutes of having
  observed the light, the witness was unable to ascribe it to any type of
  phenomenon he is familiar with.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          He was
  certain that the light could not have been part of the lighting system of
          <span class="GramE">

          </span>

         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:
  "Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2'>
          Georgetown,
  Texas, Friday, June 15, 2018, @ 5:05 a.m. (Central)—
          <span class="GramE">
           A
          </span>
          husband and wife were out walking, when their attention was suddenly drawn to
  a bright light, located in the northeastern sky, that appeared to be
  approaching the witnesses’ location.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          As they watched the light, they suddenly became aware that it was
  being followed by four smaller lights.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          As the first cluster passed overhead, the witnesses observed a second
  formation of lights, which were oriented relative to one another in a
  formation different from that of the first group.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The witnesses estimate that they witnessed
  50-100 individual lights in the formations that passed overhead, and the
  event lasted an estimated 25 minutes.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The husband is a former U. S. Air Force fighter pilot instructor.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          <a href="webreports/141/S141832.html">
           Witness
  Report
          </a>
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>

  Friday, June 15, 2018, @ 08:18 a.m. (Pacific)—On his way to work, an adult male

  suddenly drawn to a very bright object in the southern sky, which appeared to

          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

  disappeared from the witness’s sight.

  calls from young callers who appear to have little consideration for the
  welfare of others.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          Given the
  uniformity of the seemingly scripted lines these rude callers use when they
  call, we presume that they are being guided and directed by the contents of a
  foolish video posted on YouTube, urging them to call various telephone
          <span class="GramE">
           number
          </span>
          and make themselves as obnoxious as they possibly
  can.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

  Hotline if, and only if, they sincerely believe they have been witness to an
  apparently genuine UFO.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

  parents and grandparents to supervise their children’s use of cell phones and

         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          Although we have screened the reports as
  carefully as we are able to do, there is always the possibility that we may
  have overlooked a flawed report.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          As a
  result, since flawed, and even hoaxed, reports are always a possibility, we
  encourage visitors to our site to be on the lookout for defective, or
  misleading, reports.

         <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal">
          <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:
  "Times New Roman";color:#00B0F0'>
           MADAR REPORTS
           <o:p>
           </o:p>
          </span>
         </b>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          Over the past several weeks, our Center has begun
  a co-operative arrangement with Mr. Francis Ridge, long-time UFO researcher,
  Director of the National Investigations Committee on Aerial Phenomena
  (“NICAP”), and inventor of a UFO detection system, called “MADAR.”
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The term, “MADAR,” is an acronym for
  “Multiple Anomaly Detection and Automated Recording.”
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          A MADAR unit is designed to detect magnetic
  anomalies that appear to be associated with the presence of UFOs.
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          The purpose in posting the periodic detection events,
  recorded by approximately 25-30 MADAR units currently in operation around the
  world, is to address whether eyewitness sightings of suspected UFOs might be
  able to be corroborated by magnetic anomalies recorded by one, or more, MADAR
  unit(s).
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          More information about MADAR, and how it works,
  can be found at the
          <a href="http://www.nicap.org/madar.htm">
           MADAR website
          </a>
          .
  MADAR units can be purchased by contacting Mr. Ridge, whose contact
  information is available on the website shown above.
          <o:p>
          </o:p>

  and it passed overhead, providing him with a very good view of the object’s ventral

           </o:p>
          </span>
         </b>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          The NUFORC website has been updated as of this
  date, with the posting of 70 sighting reports that have been either received,
  or revised, since our last update on Friday, March 23rd, 2018.
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          Many of the posted reports have been submitted by
  sources who elect to remain totally anonymous, and/or who have provided no
  contact information with their reports.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          Consequently, we always caution visitors to our website to be on the
  constant alert for potentially falsified reports.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          We have attempted to label those reports
  that are from anonymous sources, as well as hose reports that, because of
  content, appear to our staff to address objects that probably are something
  other than authentic UFOs.
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>

  "Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2'>
          North Bend,
  Washington, Sunday, March 11, 2018, @ 04:15 a.m. (Pacific)—An adult male and
  an adult passenger, who were driving eastbound on Interstate 90 toward North
  Bend, witnessed two, seemingly rectangular, very bright lights appear their
  vehicle in the passing lane.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          Before
  the driver could move to a lane to a lane to the right, the lights suddenly
  seemed to simply disappear.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The
  highway was devoid of all other traffic.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

  "Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2'>
          Arizona (above;
  while in-flight), Monday, March 12, 2018, @ 4:05 p.m. (Mountain)—A husband
  and wife witness a strange looking object next to their aircraft, somewhere
  above Arizona.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The object appeared dark
  in color, and it appeared to the husband to be capable of changing its
  shape.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          It appeared to move in “…an
  undulating fashion
          <span class="GramE">
           ,…
          </span>
          the way a snake slithers.”
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>

  have been within 100 feet of their aircraft.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>

  seen the object, as well.

          Sunbury,
  Pennsylvania, Thursday, March 22nd, 2018, @ 9:15 p.m. (Eastern)—An adult male
  driver and his passenger suddenly become aware of the fact that their vehicle
  was being approached very rapidly by a bright light, that was directly ahead
  of them.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          As the lights got closer,
  they split into two lights, and then split again into four lights, which
  “filled the sky” ahead of their vehicle.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          Two of the lights appeared to execute a 90-degree turn and streak off,
  disappearing in the distance.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The
  other two lights suddenly did the same, following the path that the first two
  lights had taken.

           Witness Report
          </a>

  "Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2'>
          Moody, Texas,
  ~December 23rd, 1949, @ ~07:30 a.m.—Three youngsters…a 7-year old boy, his
  17-year old sister, and her 17-year old female classmate…were walking to
  school on a snowy morning, when they suddenly witnessed a silver-colored,
  disc-shaped craft, which was sitting on the ground in an empty lot.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The witness estimates the disc was
  approximately 40 in diameter, and 14 feet tall at its center, and it was
  sitting on a cylindrically shaped pedestal, approximately 3 feet in diameter.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The children then witnessed three humanoid
  creatures beneath the craft.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          The
  source of the report is a retired medical professional, with multiple
  advanced degrees.

        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal">
          <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:
  "Times New Roman";color:#00B0F0'>
           NEW UFO TELEPHONE HOTLINE POLICY
           <o:p>
           </o:p>
          </span>
         </b>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          Because of a continuing problem with a large
  volume of prank calls being placed to our UFO Hotline by young callers, we
  have had to change our policies regarding how we answer incoming calls.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          For the time being, unless we recognize,
  using “Caller ID,” the telephone number of an incoming call, we will not
  answer the call with a human operator, and will allow the call to go directly
  to our telephone messaging service.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          If
  serious-minded callers would like a return call, we invite them to leave a
  responsible-sounding message, and we will return all legitimate calls as
  quickly as we are able to do.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          In addition, we will not answer any incoming call
  which “Caller ID” indicates has been placed from a “Private Caller,” a
  “Private Number,” from an “Unknown Name,” or from a “spoofed,” i.e.
  synthetic, telephone number.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          Instead,
  we will allow such incoming calls, again, to go directly to our answering
  service, from which frivolous calls will be deleted, before we place any return
  calls.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2'>
          We apologize for any inconvenience this new
  policy may cause for responsible people attempting to contact our Center for
  legitimate purposes, but we have become fed up with ill-mannered young people
  who are using their telephones to inconvenience other people’s lives.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          It leads us to conclude that parents should
  be monitoring closely their children’s use of cell telephones, just as they
  should carefully monitor their use of computers that are connected to the
  internet.
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>

        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style="font-size:10.0pt;color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:
  bold">
          We would like to apologize to all those individuals who regularly visit
  our website, and who have become accustomed to updates to the site on at
  least a weekly basis.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          Due to some
  serious computer problems, combined with several days of out-of-town travel for
  live presentations, our last update was January 18, 2018.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          We now have the computer problems resolved,
  so we should be back to our normal schedule of weekly updates of the website.
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="style18" style="mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
         <span style="font-size:10.0pt;color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:
  bold">
          With this update, we have posted 176
          <span class="GramE">
           new,
          </span>
          or
  newly revised reports.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          Given the heavy
  volume of prank calls we are receiving over our Hotline, we suspect that
  there may well be a few written reports submitted via our Online Report Form
  that are attempts to hoax the readers.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          Hence, we caution readers to be on the alert for reports that seem
  somewhat suspicious, and in particular, those reports that have been
  submitted by anonymous sources.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </p>

         <span style="font-size:10.0pt;color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:
  bold">
          Given that we are updating tonight under a bit of time pressure, we
  have not included with this posting any photos, videos, or highlighted
  reports.
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

          We will post again soon, at
  which time we will include some graphics, together with discussion of some of
  the more interesting recent sightings.

         <span class="GramE">

         </span>

  cloudless sky, for approximately an hour.

  report.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

  the objects might have been seagulls soaring in upwelling wind, but the
  objects do not appear to look, or behave, like birds.

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Olive Branch,
  Mississippi, Tuesday, January 02nd, 2018, @ 6:38 a.m. (CST)—A husband and
  wife, while driving on Highway 78, witness two cylindrical objects pass
  across the face of an almost full Moon.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         The husband is a very experienced pilot, with approximately 22,000
  hours of flight time.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Here is the
  report submitted by the wife:
         <o:p>
         </o:p>

       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:1.0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:
  background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         BEGIN WITNESS STATEMENT:
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         “Two cylinder type objects or shadows
  traversing over full “wolf” moon Jan. 2, 2018.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:1.0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:
  background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         On Jan. 2, 2018, my husband (former airline
  pilot with 22,000 hours) and I were traveling on Lamar Ext. (Hwy. 78), coming
  out of Olive Branch, Mississippi to Memphis.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Just before the Tennessee line, I witnessed two cylindrical objects or
  shadows moving vertically over the face of a full wolf moon.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:
  background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         My husband viewed one, and I viewed
  both.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         #2 was higher than #1.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>

  face of the moon and could no longer be seen when he observed #1.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>

  of the bright face of the moon, they were no longer visible.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:
  background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Today, at 10:20 AM, while traveling
  south bound on U.S. Highway 14, approximately between Avenues D and E, an
  object was spotted at an estimated distance of ¼ mile above the highway.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         First impressions were that it was a large
  bird, like a duck or sea gull.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         As I
  kept my attention on the object, it became clear to me that it was not a bird,
  but perhaps an aircraft.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>

  background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>

  two hundred feet ahead of my car, and moving alongside the highway about 150
  feet parallel to the highway.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         As the
  object flies by my right hand view moving straight with a speed less than my
  65 MPH, I can now see that it’s an object about fifty feet in altitude.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>

  appearing smooth, and not a conventional aircraft.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Pocatello, Idaho, June 24th,
  2002, @ 8:00 p.m.—A very experienced pilot witnessed a strange-looking object
  pass below his aircraft at high speed.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         The object looked generally like the Space Shuttle, with no prominent
  wings, and appeared to the witness to be hugging the contour of the
  mountainous region below.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         It quickly
  disappeared from sight, within 15 seconds of the pilot’s first sighting of
  it.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <a href="webreports/137/S137883.html">
          Witness Report
         </a>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Albuquerque/Santa Fe
  (Waldo Canyon), New Mexico, December 14, 2017, @ 7:00 p.m.—A husband and wife
  were driving home to Santa Fe, when they both witnessed a triangular-shaped
  craft
         <span class="GramE">
          pass
         </span>
         across the highway in front of their
  vehicle.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         They agreed that the edges of
  the craft were lined with distinctly green lights, and they estimated that it
  was moving at approximately 100 miles per hour.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         The wife has provided a nice illustration
  of the peculiar object.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <a href="webreports/137/S137810.html">
          Witness Report
         </a>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          U. S.
  AIR FORCE ANNOUNCEMENT ABOUT DECEMBER 09TH EVENT OVER THE U.S.
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         For the past 12 days,
  NUFORC has received reports of an event that occurred across the U. S. on
  Saturday night, December 09th, 2017.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Our initial reaction to the reports was that they addressed a very
  unusual event, possibly UFO-related, although the U. S. Air Force has
  asserted that the sightings were of a flight of military aircraft involved in
  a large-scale nighttime training operation.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         In the interest of sharing accurate, and complete, information with
  visitors to our website,
         <a href="http://www.amc.af.mil/News/Article-Display/Article/1398050/jb-charleston-supports-usaf-weapons-school-capstone-exercise/">
          here
  is the recent USAF statement
         </a>
         .
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         However, given what we
  continue to believe are facts that, on the face of them, appear to contravene
  the Air Force explanation, we intend to continue both collecting reports, and
  investigating some of the peculiar aspects of the large-scale event.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         There are many elements of the apparent
  military exercise that simply do not seem to correlate with what many eyewitnesses
  have reported to our Center.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We have updated the
  NUFORC website as of this date, with the posting of 65 new, and 39 recently
  revised, sighting reports.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We always recommend to
  visitors to our website to be on the alert for errors and hoaxed reports,
  among the newly posted material.  Please be particularly discriminating
  when reading those reports that have been submitted by witnesses who elect to
  remain anonymous, and/or who provide no contact information, all of which we
  have attempted to label.  Many such reports appear to be high-quality,
  and probably are reliable, but some are suspect, in our opinion, so please be
  on the alert as you read them.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         UPDATE ON THE EVENTS OF
  SATURDAY NIGHT, DECEMBER 09, 2017
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We hurriedly updated
  the NUFORC website on Sunday, December 10
         <sup>
          th
         </sup>
         , in order to bring to
  the attention of the public the seemingly quite dramatic, and mysterious,
  event that appears to have taken place above, and across, the U. S. on
  Saturday night, December 09
         <sup>
          th
         </sup>
         , 2017.  For the preliminary
  details about that event, please see that earlier posting below, which was
  written on Sunday afternoon, the day after the event had occurred, and before
  we had developed a good understanding of what had taken place.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>

  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <b>
         <span style='font-size:14.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
  color:#00B0F0'>
          MAJOR EVENTS OVER THE U. S. ON SATURDAY NIGHT, DECEMBER 09TH,
  2017
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         On Saturday afternoon,
  at approximately 4:47 p.m. (Pacific), our Center began to receive the first
  of what ultimately turned out to be a large number of written and telephoned
  reports from across the U.
         <span class="GramE">
          S..
         </span>
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Most of the witnesses described allegedly
  having witnessed one, or more, large clusters of red lights, seen passing
  through the night sky at what most people described as a slow rate.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         No witnesses reported seeing green lights,
  which would have been expected, had the objects been any type of conventional
  aircraft.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Reports were received,
  in rapid sequence from the following states, in the approximate order in
  which they appear:
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Florida (?); South
  Carolina; Illinois; Missouri; Kansas; Colorado; Utah; Wyoming; Montana;
  Idaho; Washington (?); and California.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Other reports are still arriving at our Center, so we suspect that the
  objects may have been seen in other states, as well.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         One report was submitted from the U.K., and
  we are attempting to contact that source, in order to confirm that the report
  is sincere.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We hope to have all of
  the written reports posted to our website this afternoon, although our
  webmaster and his wife, who live in the Montecito area of Santa Barbara,
  California, are under alert to have to abandon their house, if the fires
  there get closer to them, so it may be a while before we can post all of the
  reports we’ve received, to date, that pertain to the sightings on the night
  of December 09th.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We will update the
  database, with all the new reported sightings, as soon as we can.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         However, we would like
  to encourage everyone who may have witnessed those clusters of lights to
  prepare a detailed statement about their sighting(s), and submit it, using
  the Online Report Form on our website, www.ufocenter.com.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We would like the witness to include where
  he or she was located, what direction the witnesses were looking, how big the
  lights appeared to be, how big the cluster of lights appeared to be, how fast
  the objects were moving across the sky, and all other details that would
  allow another person to understand clearly what the event looked like.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Please bear in mind that the more
  information included in the report, the easier it will be for another person
  to understand what the event looked like.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We look forward to your written report!!
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>

  woman, who describes herself as a retired medical professional, witnessed one

  coincides with many other estimates of the estimated sizes of the objects

        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          NUISANCE
  TELEPHONE CALLS
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         On, or about, August
  26th, 2017, our Center began receiving a substantial volume of prank
  telephone calls over its Hotline, sometimes hundreds per day, principally
  from rude, inconsiderate, and often foul-mouthed young callers.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Although the volume of calls has subsided
  to a small degree, the problem still continues, and it has compelled us to
  alter the manner in which we use the UFO Hotline.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Within the next several
  days, we will post to our homepage guidelines regarding the use of the
  Hotline, so that sincere callers will know what to expect when they telephone
  our Center.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We apologize in advance to
  those serious-minded callers who may feel inconvenienced by our new
  guidelines, but we feel we have little choice in the matter.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We simply do not have the ability
        </span>

  bold'>
         Stanley, New Mexico, Thursday, November 30th, 2017, @ 6:25 p.m.
  (MST)—An adult female, while driving south on Highway 41 in the city limits
  of Stanley, NM, witnessed a bright red light approach rapidly from her right,
  and pass almost directly overhead.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         She
  believed that if the object had been an aircraft, it would have been
  illuminated to the degree that she should have been able to see its outline,
  but she did not see anything but the light.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>

          Witness Report
         </a>

  Thanksgiving holiday, we have update the NUFORC website
         <span class="GramE">
          on
          <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
          </span>

         </span>

  2017, with the posting of 70 new, or recently amended sighting reports.

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We urge visitors to our
  site to be discriminating, as they read the reports, given the possibility
  that some of the reports may be hoaxes.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We have attempted to label all the reports that have been submitted by
  sources who elect to remain anonymous, and/or who provide no contact
         <span class="GramE">
          information,
         </span>
         given that we suspect that those reports have
  the highest likelihood of being prank reports.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>

        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          NEW
  HOTLINE POLICY
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Because of a continuing
  deluge of prank calls that are being submitted to the NUFORC Hotline, we have
  had to curtail answering our telephone on a live, or real-time, basis, until
  the frivolous calls cease.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         If a
  serious-minded caller wishes to leave a message on the Hotline answering
  service, he or she is invited to do so, and we will attempt to return the
  call as quickly as we are able to do so.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         All other calls are deleted, and are not responded to.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         The NUFORC website has
  been updated as of Friday evening, November 17, 2017, with the posting of
  approximately 101 new reports, submitted since the afternoon of Thursday,
  November 09th.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         The newly posted
  reports have been proof-read by us, but we were under time pressure at the
  time, so there may well be mistakes, oversights, and overt hoaxes among the
  new reports, which escaped our attention.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Hence, please be
         <span class="GramE">
          remain
         </span>
         skeptical as you read
  the reports.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Here are a few of the
  reports that caught our attention:
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>

  (Pacific)—A husband, wife, and their children all witnessed two orange lights

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Dewey, Arizona, Wednesday,
  November 15, 2017, @ 9:00 p.m. (Mountain)—A gentleman who describes himself
  as a retired engineer, reports witnessing the sudden appearance of three
  “chevron” shaped objects, each bearing individual marker lights, suddenly
  appeared in the night sky.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         The
  objects’ apparent width was approximately the diameter of a full Moon, and
  each “chevron” exhibited its own individual “marker” lights.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         The objects simply appeared out of nowhere,
  one after the other, and then disappeared instantly, in a similar
  manner.

         </span>

          Witness Report

         The NUFORC website has
  been updated, as of this date, November 09th, 2017, with the posting of 78
  recently received sighting reports, submitted since the afternoon of Friday,
  November 03rd, 2017
         <o:p>
         </o:p>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Given the high volume
  of prank telephone calls that are being placed to our telephone Hotline, we
  suspect that the same phenomenon may be spilling over to our Online Report
  Form.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Consequently, we feel duty-bound
  to caution visitors to our site from accepting everything that is posted
  there, suspecting that some of the reports, particularly those from anonymous
  sources, may be attempts to slip hoaxed reports and pranks past our editing
  process.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Those reports from anonymous
  sources have been labeled.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We have updated our
  website, as of this date, Friday, November 03rd, 2017, with the posting of
  222 new reports, received since the afternoon of October 19th.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         In addition, we have included in the
  posting 19 reports that have been revised, since their original posting.
         <o:p>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         All of the new reports
  have been proof-read by us before this posting, but we have not had the time
  this week to read them as carefully as we traditionally like to do.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         As a result, we suspect that there are many
  reports that have flaws in them, particularly with regard to the time and
  date of the reported incidents.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         In
  addition, some of the reports may be overt attempts to hoax us, and the
  visitors to our website, so we encourage those individuals who read the
  reports to be on the alert for errors in the reports.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;

  updated twice during the past week, with postings on Thursday, September
  21st, and then a week later, on September 28th, 2017.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We have posted approximately 240 reports,
  collected, in aggregate, since September 14th.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

        </span>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Given that our center
  continues to be inundated with prank telephone calls over its Hotline, we
  assume that some of the same people who are placing those nuisance calls may
  be submitting hoaxed written reports, as well.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Hence, we encourage visitors to our website
  to be discriminating in reading the reports in our database of sightings, and
  believing everything written there at face value.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         REPORTS OF CLUSTERS OF
  “ORBS” AND “FIREBALLS”
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         In May 2012, our
  Center, and other UFO organizations, as well, began receiving large numbers
  of reports of red, orange, or yellow “orbs,” or “fireballs.”
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         This phenomenon has continued over the past
  five years, and seems not to have abated in the least during that time.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         The date of this posting, September 28th,
  marks the fourth anniversary of what our staff considers to have been one of
  the most dramatic such sightings, which was reported to our Center by a
  retired Arizona Highway Patrol, who resides in Glendale, AZ, a suburb on the
  northwest corner of Phoenix, AZ.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         In
  order to underscore the unusual nature of the reports of “fireballs,” we
  revisit that case here:
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;
  margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l32 level1 lfo18;
  mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;mso-element-wrap:around;

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  "Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:
  bold'>
         Glendale, Arizona, Saturday, September 28, 2013, @ 7:15 p.m.
  (Mountain)—
         <span class="GramE">
          A
         </span>
         former Arizona Highway Patrol officer
  describes his shock in witnessing an orange “orb” of light, that streaks from
  west to east in the northern sky.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         He
  quickly walks out to a porch on the northern side of the house, hoping to get
  a final glimpse of the peculiar object, as it disappeared to the east.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Over the next several minutes, he witnessed
  another approximately 150 similar objects, which he estimated moved across
  the sky at approximately 150-200 miles per hour.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <a href="webreports/102/S102803.html">
          Witness
  Report
         </a>

  adult male, standing on his daughter’s roof to assess recent wind damage,
  sees two highly reflective objects in the clear, cloudless sky.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">

  photograph of the two objects and also provided the drawing shown.

        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          NUFORC
  WEBSITE UPDATED ON TUESDAY, SEPTEMBER 12, 2017
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Although NUFORC usually
  updates its
         <span class="GramE">
          website,
         </span>
         and database of sighting
  reports, on Thursdays or Fridays, we have accelerated that schedule this week
  because of Peter Davenport’s scheduled appearance tonight as a guest on the
  internet based Coast to Coast “Insider” program.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We thought it would be helpful to the
  program’s subscribers to have the latest reports posted, in order to invite
  comments about recent sightings and events.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>

  8:00 p.m. (Pacific) on Tuesday night, September 12, 2017, and Coast to Coast
  AM host, George
         <span class="SpellE">
          Noory
         </span>
         , will field questions during
  the first half hour, followed by Peter during the second half of the program.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>

         We highlight below a
  few recent reports:
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>

       <p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;
  margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l12 level1 lfo20;
  mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;mso-element-wrap:around;
  mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:margin;
  mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;
  mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2;
  mso-bidi-font-weight:bold">
         <span style="mso-list:Ignore">
          ·
          <span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  "Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:
  bold'>
         Monroe, Michigan, Saturday, September 09th, 2017, @ 10:30 p.m.
  (Eastern)—An adult male observer witnessed an estimated 8-12 unidentified red
  “orbs” drift across the nighttime sky.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Witness provides a high-quality illustration of the event.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         NOTE:
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         NUFORC has chosen to highlight this case, principally because it is so
  similar to many other similar cases, involving the sighting of clusters of
  red, orange, or yellow “fireballs,” or “orbs.”
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         This type of sighting appears to have
  increased in frequency, beginning sometime during the month of May 2012, and
  it has continued unabated.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <a href="webreports/136/S136100.html">
          Witness Report
         </a>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;
  margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:.5in;text-indent:-.25in;mso-list:l12 level1 lfo20;

  mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:margin;

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  "Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:
  bold'>
         Tinley Park, Illinois, Saturday, July 30, 2016, @ 21:00 hrs.
  (Central)—An adult female reports having witnessed an estimated 25 to 35
  “red-orange” self-luminous objects pass slowly overhead.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <a href="webreports/136/S136123.html">
          Witness
  Report
         </a>
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         NOTE:
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Tinley Park, and nearby Orland Park,
  Illinois, were the site of similar sightings on August 21st, and October
  31st, 2004.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>

        <i style="mso-bidi-font-style:normal">
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:

          Posted on Tuesday afternoon, September 12, 2017.

       <div style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-bottom:12.0pt">
        <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:center;mso-element:frame;
  mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:
  paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:margin;mso-element-left:center;

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          NUFORC
  HOMEPAGE UPDATED ON SEPTEMBER 05TH AND SEPTEMBER 08, 2017
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Over the past three
  days, we have updated our website on two occasions, with the posting, in
  aggregate, of approximately 200 new, and recently amended, reports, received
  since our last posting on August 24th.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         This September 8th
  posting will be abbreviated, given that we are a bit pressed for time at the
  time of this update, but we will post again within the next several days, in
  order to include photographs we’ve received recently, as well as to highlight
  several very nice reports that have captured our attention.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We always issue a
  warning to visitors to be on the lookout for flawed or prank reports, and
  that warning is particularly pertinent in this posting, given the statement
  which follows below.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We suspect that
  many of the people who have submitted prank calls to our Hotline probably
  have also submitted pranked reports.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          LARGE
  VOLUME OF PRANK CALLS TO OUR HOTLINE – YOU CAN HELP!
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Beginning on Saturday,
  August 26th, our Center began receiving a large volume of overtly pranked
  calls over its Hotline, as many as 100-150 per day!
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         What immediately caught our attention was
  the fact that virtually all of the calls were being placed by young children,
  as young, we estimate, as perhaps 8 years of age, and as old as perhaps 13 or
  14 year.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Moreover, what we find
  equally noteworthy was the fact that all of the prank calls are virtually the
  same, as if the children were being coached on how to conduct themselves
  during the their respective calls to the Hotline.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         When they call, for example, the young
  callers often say nothing, simply hanging on the telephone, while remaining
  totally mute.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         In the rare occasions
  when they actually speak during their call, they usually use a
         <span class="GramE">
          pseudonym,
         </span>
         or babel some mishmash of unintelligible
  nonsense.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         In addition, they are
  generally evasive, and when queried as to where they had learned of our
  website, they studiously avoid responding, again, remaining mute.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         The calls are almost “cookie cutter” like,
  which we find to be both noteworthy, and unsettling.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         After some
  investigation, we have discovered that the problem appears to be the result
  of a video posted to YouTube, inviting its many young followers to harass our
  Center with prank calls:
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Many of our friends
  have expressed their displeasure with the offending posted video by voting to
  have it removed from YouTube’s website.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         We invite anyone who would like to assist us in this effort to cast
  their vote for removal of the offending website by casting their vote via the
  process created by YouTube site for just such a circumstance, and which we
  outline below:
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=BXXaMcqSGDI">
          The video is here.
         </a>
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         When you get to the page, press the icons
  shown below to down vote the video and report it as abusive.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Thank you!
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>

  paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:margin;mso-element-left:center;
  mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;
  font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;mso-themecolor:background2;
  mso-no-proof:yes'>

  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         <o:p>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:

        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          RADIO
  APPEARANCE

          </o:p>

        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Peter Davenport, NUFORC
  Director, will make his weekly appearance on the Coast to Coast AM radio
  program, hosted by George
         <span class="SpellE">
          Noory
         </span>
         , on Friday night,
  September 08th, 2017, at approximately 10:15 p.m. (Pacific).
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         He will discuss some recent sightings, and
  may discuss the problem of prank calls to our Hotline.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We have updated our
  website, as of this date, with the posting of 117 new, and newly revised,
  sighting reports.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         As we do with every
  update, we encourage visitors to our site to be on the alert for
         <span class="GramE">
          flawed,
         </span>
         or hoaxed reports, among not only the new reports,
  but among those that have been posted to our site for some time.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          SOLAR
  ECLIPSE AND UFO SIGHTINGS
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         For some reason that
  escapes our understanding, some people believe that there is an above-average
  likelihood of experiencing a UFO sighting during an eclipse, either solar or
  lunar, than there is at any other time of day or night.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Our Center fails to see any objective
  evidence to support this claim, and the recent solar eclipse that occurred on
  August 21st, 2017, seems to provide support for our belief.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         People may, in fact
  experience what they believe was a sighting of a UFO during an eclipse, but
  the reports submitted to NUFORC for events that occurred during the recent
  eclipse suggest to use that they are no more likely to occur than they are at
  any other time.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Our Center received 20
  reports for August 21st, 2017, a few of which appeared to have occurred at
  times when the local solar disc was in some degree of eclipse, but most of
  the reports appear to us to involve photographic “lens flares,” captured when
  people pointed their cameras directly at the Sun.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         Obviously, such photographic “ghost” images
  have nothing to do with legitimate sightings of authentic UFOs.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <b>
         <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#00B0F0'>
          NOTEWORTHY
  CASES
          <o:p>
          </o:p>
         </span>
        </b>
       </p>

  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>

         Ft. Mill, South Carolina, Friday, August 11, 2017 @ 22:57 hrs. (EDT) -
  Two adult

        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We have posted 144
  recently submitted, or recently revised, sighting reports to our database of
  cases, as of the afternoon of this date.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>

       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         We have proof-read the
  reports as carefully as our time allows, but there is always the likelihood
  that we have overlooked errors in the reports.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         With every posting, we are in the habit of
  encouraging visitors to our website to be on the alert for reports that
  appear to address something other than apparent UFO-related incidents.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         As we comb through the reports, we are
  constantly on the look-out for incidents related to reflections of the Sun
  from “Iridium” satellites; overflights of the International Space Station
  (“ISS”), and of other satellites; missile launches from Florida, California,
  and Virginia; sightings of stars and planets, etc., and we detect many of
  those types of incidents, but usually not all of them.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
       </p>
       <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:
  12.0pt;margin-left:0in;mso-element:frame;mso-element-frame-hspace:9.0pt;
  mso-element-wrap:around;mso-element-anchor-vertical:paragraph;mso-element-anchor-horizontal:
  margin;mso-element-left:center;mso-element-top:1.35pt;mso-height-rule:exactly">
        <span style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#EEECE1;
  mso-themecolor:background2;mso-bidi-font-weight:bold'>
         Hence, as visitors read
  through the reports, we encourage them to always be skeptical, and to be
  alert for flawed reports, including possible hoaxes.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         In particular, be skeptical of those
  reports from individuals who elect to remain anonymous.
         <span style="mso-spacerun:yes">
         </span>
         If you discover what you believe may be a
  defective or misleading report, please send a notification to
  director@ufocenter.com, and we will review the situation, at our earliest
  convenience.
         <o:p>
         </o:p>
        </span>
